## FAQs

**Which graduate jobs & internships can I still apply for right now?**
Many structured graduate schemes and summer internships run on annual cycles — but a large share of employers recruit on a **rolling basis**, and graduate *jobs*, apprenticeships, trades, sales and entry-level roles run year-round. This list shows what's **live today**, refreshed daily.

**What's an assessment centre and how do I prepare?**
A half- to two-day mix of group exercises, presentations, in-tray tasks and interviews — usually the final stage. See [interview & assessment tips on Workopia](https://workopia.io/resources/interview-tips?utm_source=github&utm_medium=repo&utm_campaign=us-new-grad-internship-jobs).

**How do I get alerts for new roles?**
Set a job alert on Workopia by role + city and we'll email you when new US roles go live — [start here](https://workopia.io/browsejobs/positions/us/graduate-program?utm_source=github&utm_medium=repo&utm_campaign=us-new-grad-internship-jobs).
